msg:I brought my family here, booked three rooms, and just pasted and copied the text! I brought my children to see the adults soaking in hot springs, climbing Xiling Snow Mountain, and riding the ropeway. I have to say that the hotelâ€™s hot springs are as good as ever. I have been to Xiling Snow Mountain five times since graduating from college, and stayed here three times. This hotel is convenient for hot spring bathing. The air is good and the mountains are fresh. Especially in the morning, the air is very good and the scenery is good. There are many hot springs. Choose a small one and soak in it yourself for a unique flavor.
Hygiene: But I have to remind you about the hotel room. As soon as you enter the door, there is a stuffy musty smell. Maybe there is a hot spring behind it, but you still need to ventilate it more. The balcony door is closed. The smell is a bit heavy and stuffy as soon as you enter.
There are places for shopping around the hotel. There are many places to eat, which are delicious. There is also an extra place for feeding pigeons, which is quite good.
